country_event = { # Manchuria wants to form an alliance
	id = fengtian.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.2"}
	title = fengtian.2.t
	desc = fengtian.2.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = fengtian.2.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 95 }

		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction = no }

			create_faction = "Asian Co-Prosperity Sphere"
		}

		add_to_faction = FNG
		add_political_power = 60
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FNG modifier = JAP_ALL_FNG } # 100
	}

	option = {
		name = fengtian.2.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 5 }

		add_political_power = -20
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FNG modifier = JAP_NO_ALL_FNG } # -100
	}
}

country_event = { # Zhang Zuolin's Betrayal
	id = fengtian.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.3"}
	title = fengtian.3.t
	desc = fengtian.3.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = fengtian.3.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }

		declare_war_on = { target = FNG type = annex_everything	}
		end_puppet = FNG
		hidden_effect = { FNG = { country_event = { id = fengtian.17 days = 1 }}}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_2
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = FNG_Post-Colonial_Chaos_1
				days = 30
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_3
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = FNG_Post-Colonial_Chaos_1
				days = 60
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_4
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = FNG_Post-Colonial_Chaos_2
				days = 45
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_5
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = FNG_Post-Colonial_Chaos_3
				days = 45
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = mantetsu_industrial_subsiduaries
			}
			remove_ideas = {
				mantetsu_industrial_subsiduaries
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = mitsubishi_heavy_industries
			}
			remove_ideas = {
				mitsubishi_heavy_industries
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = fengtian.3.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 10 }

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_war_with = GER
				NOT = {
					is_in_faction_with = FRA
					is_in_faction_with = RUS
					is_in_faction_with = SOV
					is_in_faction_with = USA
					is_in_faction_with = CAN
				}
			}

			hidden_effect = { GER = { country_event = { id = fengtian.17 days = 1 }}}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = fengtian.3.c

		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }

		add_political_power = -60
	}
}

country_event = { # Zhang Zuolin has refused to fight!
	id = fengtian.4
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.4"}
	title = fengtian.4.t
	desc = fengtian.4.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = fengtian.4.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 60 }

		hidden_effect = { FNG = { country_event = { id = fengtian.7 days = 1 }}}
	}

	option = {
		name = fengtian.4.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }

		add_political_power = -60
	}

	option = {
		name = fengtian.4.c

		ai_chance = { factor = 20 }

		declare_war_on = { target = FNG type = annex_everything	}
		end_puppet = FNG
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_2
			}
			FNG = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = FNG_Post-Colonial_Chaos_1
					days = 30
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_3
			}
			FNG = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = FNG_Post-Colonial_Chaos_1
					days = 60
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_4
			}
			FNG = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = FNG_Post-Colonial_Chaos_2
					days = 45
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_5
			}
			FNG = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = FNG_Post-Colonial_Chaos_3
					days = 45
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = mantetsu_industrial_subsiduaries
			}
			remove_ideas = {
				mantetsu_industrial_subsiduaries
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = mitsubishi_heavy_industries
			}
			remove_ideas = {
				mitsubishi_heavy_industries
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Japan seeks to negotiate
	id = fengtian.6
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.6"}
	title = fengtian.6.t
	desc = fengtian.6.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = fengtian.6.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }

		GER = { country_event = { id = fengtian.8 days = 6 }}
	}

	option = {
		name = fengtian.6.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }

		add_political_power = -60
	}
}

country_event = { # Zhang Zuolin has refused our demands
	id = fengtian.10
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.10"}
	title = fengtian.10.t
	desc = fengtian.10.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = fengtian.10.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }

		declare_war_on = { target = FNG type = annex_everything	}
		end_puppet = FNG
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_2
			}
			FNG = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = FNG_Post-Colonial_Chaos_1
					days = 30
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_3
			}
			FNG = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = FNG_Post-Colonial_Chaos_1
					days = 60
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_4
			}
			FNG = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = FNG_Post-Colonial_Chaos_2
					days = 45
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_5
			}
			FNG = {
				add_timed_idea = {
					idea = FNG_Post-Colonial_Chaos_3
					days = 45
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = mantetsu_industrial_subsiduaries
			}
			remove_ideas = {
				mantetsu_industrial_subsiduaries
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = mitsubishi_heavy_industries
			}
			remove_ideas = {
				mitsubishi_heavy_industries
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = fengtian.10.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }

		add_political_power = -60
	}

	option = {
		name = fengtian.10.c

		ai_chance = { factor = 30 }

		trigger = {
			has_war_with = JAP
		}

		JAP = { white_peace_with_ROOT = yes }

		if = {
			limit = { is_in_faction_with = GER }

			hidden_effect = { GER = { country_event = { id = fengtian.14 days = 1 }}}

			remove_from_faction = QIE
		}

		hidden_effect = { JAP = { country_event = { id = fengtian.16 days = 1 }}}
#		hidden_effect = { FNG = { country_event = { id = fengtian.18 days = 1 }}}
	}
}

country_event = { # We have sat down at the table
	id = fengtian.13
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.13"}
	title = fengtian.13.t
	desc = fengtian.13.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = fengtian.13.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 75 }

		GER = { white_peace_with_ROOT = yes }
		QIE = { white_peace_with_ROOT = yes }

		add_ideas = JAP_WAR_REP
		GER = { add_ideas = JAP_WAR_REP_GER }

		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = QIE }
			diplomatic_relation = { country = QIE relation = non_aggression_pact }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = GER }
			diplomatic_relation = { country = GER relation = non_aggression_pact }
		}
		add_political_power = -100
	}

	option = {
		name = fengtian.13.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }

		add_political_power = -40
	}
}

country_event = { # We have sat down at the table
	id = fengtian.14
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.14"}
	title = fengtian.14.t
	desc = fengtian.14.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = fengtian.14.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 25 }

		GER = { white_peace_with_ROOT = yes }
		QIE = { white_peace_with_ROOT = yes }

		add_ideas = JAP_WAR_REP_FULL
		GER = { add_ideas = JAP_WAR_REP_GER_FULL }

		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = QIE }
			diplomatic_relation = { country = QIE relation = non_aggression_pact }
		}
		if = {
			limit = { country_exists = GER }
			diplomatic_relation = { country = GER relation = non_aggression_pact }
		}
		add_political_power = -500

		end_puppet = PHI
		end_puppet = TRM

		GER = {
			transfer_state = 526
			transfer_state = 645
			transfer_state = 648
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = fengtian.14.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 75 }

		add_political_power = 100
	}
}

country_event = { # The Qing have abandoned us!

country_event = { # Kolchak has broken away from Japanese rule!
	id = fengtian.19
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.19"}
	title = fengtian.19.t
	desc = fengtian.19.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = FNG
		NOT = { has_global_flag = Man_puyi}
		country_exists = TRM
		has_global_flag = PRI_breaksaway
		TRM = { is_subject = no }
		is_subject_of = JAP
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}

	option = {
		name = fengtian.19.a

		ai_chance = { factor = 100 }

		add_political_power = -20
		clr_global_flag = PRI_breaksaway
	}

	option = {
		name = fengtian.19.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }

		TRM = { white_peace_with_ROOT = yes }
		JAP = {
			end_puppet = FNG
		}
		hidden_effect = { TRM = { country_event = { id = fengtian.20 days = 1 }}}
		hidden_effect = { JAP = { country_event = { id = fengtian.23 days = 1 }}}
		clr_global_flag = PRI_breaksaway
	}

	option = {
		name = fengtian.19.c

		ai_chance = { factor = 0 }

		trigger = {
			country_exists = QIE
			QIE = { is_subject = no }
		}

		QIE = { white_peace_with_ROOT = yes }
		JAP = {
			end_puppet = FNG
		}
		add_political_power = -500
#		hidden_effect = { QIE = { country_event = { id = fengtian.21 days = 1 }}}
		hidden_effect = { JAP = { country_event = { id = fengtian.23 days = 1 }}}
		clr_global_flag = PRI_breaksaway
	}
}

		set_country_flag = FNG_QIE_Union

		name = fengtian.40.b

		ai_chance = { factor = 70 }

		add_opinion_modifier = { target = FNG modifier = SQI_ALL_FNG } # 50

		name = fengtian.40.c

	}

country_event = { # Two republics as one!
	id = fengtian.41
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.41"}
	title = fengtian.41.t
	desc = fengtian.41.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_spain_civil_war_soldiers

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = fengtian.41.a

		annex_country = { target = SQI transfer_troops = yes }
		add_political_power = -200
		add_opinion_modifier = { target = JAP modifier = FNG_SQI_UNION_JAP } # -150
		add_manpower = 50000

		every_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = QIE }

			add_core_of = FNG
		}

		every_state = {
			limit = { is_core_of = SQI }

			remove_core_of = SQI
		}

		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { is_in_faction_with = AOG }}

			hidden_effect = { FNG = { country_event = { id = repchi.3 days = 1 }}}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { # Imperial Fury
	id = fengtian.new.22
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.new.22"}
	title = fengtian.new.22.t
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.new.22.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					tag = FNG
					NOT = {
						FNG = {
							is_subject_of = JAP
						}
					}
					market_liberal > 0.00
					market_liberal < 0.05
				}
				AND = {
					has_global_flag = fengtian_refuses_food
					has_global_flag = japan_punishes_fengtian
				}
				has_global_flag = fengtian_blames_japan
			}
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.new.22.d_influence_low
		trigger = {
			tag = FNG
			NOT = {
				AND = {
					has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_1
					has_country_flag = fengtian_refuses_food
				}
			}
			market_liberal > 0.00
			market_liberal < 0.05
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.new.22.d_fengtian_refuses_food
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = fengtian_refuses_food
			has_global_flag = japan_punishes_fengtian
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fengtian.new.22.d_fengtian_blames_japan
		trigger = {
			has_global_flag = fengtian_blames_japan
		}
	}
	picture = japan_ultimatum

	fire_only_once = no

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 7
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = FNG
		NOT = {
			has_completed_focus = FNG_Expel_Japanese_Officers
			has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_1
			has_country_flag = japan_aid_cut
		}
		OR = {
			AND = {
				market_liberal > 0.00
				market_liberal < 0.05
			}
			has_global_flag = fengtian_refuses_food
		}
	}

	option = { #A hard lesson
		name = fengtian.new.22.a
		add_political_power = -100
		add_ideas = FNG_Japanese_Aid_Cut
		set_country_flag = japan_aid_cut
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = 0.10
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CAPOP_10
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 85
		}
	}

	option = { #A perfect time to strike!
		name = fengtian.new.22.b
		trigger = {
			has_war = no
		}
		add_political_power = 200
		remove_from_faction = FNG
		JAP = {
			end_puppet = FNG
		}
		declare_war_on = {
			target = JAP
			type = annex_everything
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = -100.00
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CAPOP_-100
		add_ideas = FNG_informal_empire_1
		JAP = {
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = JAP_MANTETSU_COLLAPSE
				days = 235
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 15
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_2
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = FNG_Post-Colonial_Chaos_1
				days = 35
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_3
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = FNG_Post-Colonial_Chaos_1
				days = 65
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_4
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = FNG_Post-Colonial_Chaos_2
				days = 50
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_5
			}
			add_timed_idea = {
				idea = FNG_Post-Colonial_Chaos_3
				days = 50
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = mantetsu_industrial_subsiduaries
			}
			remove_ideas = {
				mantetsu_industrial_subsiduaries
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = mitsubishi_heavy_industries
			}
			remove_ideas = {
				mitsubishi_heavy_industries
			}
		}
	}

	title = fengtian.new.61.t
	desc = fengtian.new.61.d
	picture = japan_science

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = FNG
		has_country_flag = chosabu_radar
		JAP = {
			has_tech = radio_detection
		}
		FNG = {
			is_subject_of = JAP
		}
		NOT = {
			FNG = {
				has_tech = radio_detection
				has_tech = decimetric_radar
				has_tech = improved_decimetric_radar
				has_tech = centimetric_radar
				has_tech = improved_centimetric_radar
				has_tech = advanced_centimetric_radar
			}
		}
	}

	}

		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = radar
			bonus = 0.40
			uses = 1
			category = radar_tech
		}
	}
}

		}

	option = { #Fengtian's defenses are strong!
		name = fengtian.new.144.a
		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = 0.01
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CAPOP_1
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = yamato_hotels_limited
			}
			add_political_power = -10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_completed_focus = FNG_Modernized_Curriculum
					has_completed_focus = FNG_Fortress_Manchuria
				}
			}
			add_political_power = 20
			modify_country_flag = {
				flag = prince_impress_level
				value = 1
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_completed_focus = FNG_Modernized_Curriculum
					has_completed_focus = FNG_Fortress_Manchuria
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -20
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = prince_shot
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = fengtian.new.149
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = prince_shot
				}
				has_completed_focus = FNG_Establish_the_Jinzhou_Industrial_Zone
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = fengtian.new.145
					days = 5
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = prince_shot
					has_completed_focus = FNG_Establish_the_Jinzhou_Industrial_Zone
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				country_event = {
					id = fengtian.new.146
					days = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #It is safest to end the visit here
		name = fengtian.new.144.b
		add_political_power = -50
		add_stability = -0.05
		hidden_effect = {

				ideology = market_liberal
				popularity = -0.03
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = CAPOP_-3
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 30
		}
	}
}

				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			}
			set_country_flag = Wu_leak_fired
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_Zang_Shiyi_int_pau
			}
			add_popularity = {
				popularity = -0.03
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
			}
			set_country_flag = Zang_leak_fired
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_Tang_Yulin_int_pau
			}
			add_popularity = {
				popularity = -0.03
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
			}
			set_country_flag = Tang_leak_fired
		}
	}

	option = { #He must be removed from office!
		name = fengtian.new.172.b
		add_political_power = -20
		clr_country_flag = intel_leak
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_Wu_Jinglian_for_ade
			}
			remove_ideas = FNG_Wu_Jinglian_for_ade
			add_popularity = {
				popularity = -0.03
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			}
			set_country_flag = Wu_leak_fired
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_Zang_Shiyi_int_pau
			}
			remove_ideas = FNG_Zang_Shiyi_int_pau
			add_popularity = {
				popularity = -0.03
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
			}
			set_country_flag = Zang_leak_fired
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_Tang_Yulin_int_pau
			}
			add_popularity = {
				popularity = -0.03
				ideology = paternal_autocrat
			}
			set_country_flag = Tang_leak_fired
		}
	}
}

	id = fngpolitic.0
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fngpolitic.0"}

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

		set_country_flag = minister_nomination_available
	}

	}
}


country_event = { #Recovery League/Ade Foreign Minister
	id = fngpolitic.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fngpolitic.1"}
	title = fngpolitic.1.t
	desc = {
		text = fngpolitic.1.d_Wu
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = Wu_Jinglian_for_ade
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fngpolitic.1.d_Chang
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = Chang_Chun_for_ade
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fngpolitic.1.d_Huang
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = Huang_Fu_for_ade
		}
	}
	desc = {
		text = fngpolitic.1.d_Huang_hog
		trigger = {
			has_idea = FNG_Huang_Fu_hog_ade
			has_country_flag = Huang_Fu_for_ade
		}
	}
	picture = china_ambassador_announcement

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 10
	}

	trigger = {
		tag = FNG
		has_country_flag = minister_nomination_available
		authdem_pop_high = yes
		NOT = {
			ade_has_foreign_minister = yes
		}
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = FNG_Huang_Fu_hog_ade
				}
				random_list = {
					60 = {
						set_country_flag = Wu_Jinglian_for_ade
					}
					40 = {
						set_country_flag = Chang_Chun_for_ade
					}
				}
				else = {
					random_list = {
						50 = {
							set_country_flag = Wu_Jinglian_for_ade
						}
						30 = {
							set_country_flag = Chang_Chun_for_ade
						}
						20 = {
							set_country_flag = Huang_Fu_for_ade
						}
					}
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = minister_nomination_available
			country_event = {
				id = fngpolitic.0
				days = 130
			}
		}
	}

	option = { #Appoint Wu
		name = fngpolitic.1.a
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = Wu_Jinglian_for_ade
		}
		add_ideas = {
			FNG_Wu_Jinglian_for_ade
		}
		clr_country_flag = Chang_Chun_for_ade
		clr_country_flag = Wu_Jinglian_for_ade

		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				35 = {
					country_event = {
						id = fengtian.new.24
						days = 36
					}
				}
				35 = {
					country_event = {
						id = fengtian.new.49
						days = 28
					}
				}
				30 = {}
			}
			add_popularity = {
				popularity = 0.02
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			}
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = RLPOP_2
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					ade_has_foreign_minister = yes
					pau_has_foreign_minister = yes
					mli_has_foreign_minister = yes
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -50
			custom_effect_tooltip = FNG_one_time_cost
		}
	}

	option = { #Appoint Chang
		name = fngpolitic.1.b
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = Chang_Chun_for_ade
		}
		add_ideas = {
			FNG_Chang_Chun_for_ade
		}
		clr_country_flag = Chang_Chun_for_ade
		clr_country_flag = Wu_Jinglian_for_ade

		hidden_effect = {
			add_popularity = {
				popularity = 0.02
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			}
		}
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 70
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					ade_has_foreign_minister = yes
					pau_has_foreign_minister = yes
					mli_has_foreign_minister = yes
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -150
			custom_effect_tooltip = FNG_one_time_cost
		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = RLPOP_2
	}

	option = { #Appoint Huang
		name = fngpolitic.1.c
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = Huang_Fu_for_ade
		}
		add_ideas = {
			FNG_Huang_Fu_for_ade
		}
		clr_country_flag = Chang_Chun_for_ade
		clr_country_flag = Wu_Jinglian_for_ade
		clr_country_flag = Huang_Fu_for_ade

			add_popularity = {
				popularity = 0.02
				ideology = authoritarian_democrat
			}
		}

			factor = 70
		}
		if = {

				NOT = {

					pau_has_foreign_minister = yes
					mli_has_foreign_minister = yes
				}
			}
			add_political_power = -150

		}
		custom_effect_tooltip = RLPOP_2
	}

	option = { #Refuse to Appoint

		add_stability = -0.01

		clr_country_flag = Wu_Jinglian_for_ade
		clr_country_flag = Huang_Fu_for_ade

country_event = {
	id = fengtian.informalempire.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.informalempire.1"}
	title = fengtian.informalempire.1.t
	desc = fengtian.informalempire.1.d

	fire_only_once = no

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			remove_ideas = {
				FNG_informal_empire_2
				FNG_informal_empire_3
				FNG_informal_empire_4
				FNG_informal_empire_5
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = fengtian.informalempire.1.a
		add_ideas = FNG_informal_empire_1
	}
}

### Informal Empire 2 - Preservation of the Xinhai Order
country_event = {
	id = fengtian.informalempire.2
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.informalempire.2"}
	title = fengtian.informalempire.2.t
	desc = fengtian.informalempire.2.d

	fire_only_once = no

	trigger = {
		tag = FNG
		has_completed_focus = FNG_Preservation_of_the_Xinhai_Order
		NOT = { has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_2 }
		market_liberal > 0.01
		market_liberal < 0.19
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}

	option = {
		name = fengtian.informalempire.2.a
		swap_ideas = {
			remove_idea = FNG_informal_empire_3
			add_idea = FNG_informal_empire_2
		}
	}
}

### Informal Empire 3 - Mantetsu Influence
country_event = {
	id = fengtian.informalempire.3
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fengtian.informalempire.3"}
	title = fengtian.informalempire.3.t
	desc = fengtian.informalempire.3.d

	picture = anshan_steel

	fire_only_once = no

	trigger = {
		tag = FNG
		NOT = { has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_3 }
		market_liberal > 0.20
		market_liberal < 0.30
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 2
	}

	option = {
		name = fengtian.informalempire.3.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_2
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = FNG_informal_empire_2
				add_idea = FNG_informal_empire_3
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_idea = FNG_informal_empire_4
			}
			swap_ideas = {
				remove_idea = FNG_informal_empire_4
				add_idea = FNG_informal_empire_3
			}
		}
	}
}

	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fngwar.0"}

	hidden = yes

	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		set_country_flag = fng_war_available
	}

	option = {
	}
}

country_event = { # Qing Pre-War
	id = fngwar.1
	immediate = {log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event fngwar.1"}
	title = fngwar.1.t
	desc = fngwar.1.d

	fire_only_once = yes

	trigger = {
		tag = FNG
		has_country_flag = fng_war_available
		country_exists = QIE
		FNG = {
			is_neighbor_of = QIE
			has_war = no
			is_subject = yes
			has_completed_focus = FNG_Begin_the_War_of_National_Reclamation
		}
	}

	mean_time_to_happen = {
		days = 150
	}


	option = {
		name = fngwar.1.a
		create_wargoal = {
			type = annex_everything
			target = QIE
		}
		country_event = {
			days = 48
			id = fngwar.2
		}
		clr_country_flag = fng_war_available
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = fngwar.0
				days = 200
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = fngwar.1.b
		add_political_power = -50
		clr_country_flag = fng_war_available
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = fngwar.0
				days = 150
			}
		}
	}
}
